        <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; text-align: left; white-space: pre; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
         <span class="pln" style="border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; text-align: left; white-space: pre;">

   <div class="snippet" data-id="299" style="width:600px; height:369px; top:92px; left:671px; min-height:20px; z-index:450;">
    <div class="snippet-content">
     <div class="toolbar toolbar-top">
      <a class="remove-snippet" data-id="299" href="#">
       <i class="icon-remove">
       </i>
      </a>
      <div class="title-holder">
       <a class="origin-title" href="http://serverfault.com/questions/6269/useful-commandline-commands-on-unix">
        linux - Useful Commandline Commands on Unix - Server Fault
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-299">
       <p>
       </p>
       <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 36px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
        As there is a
        <a href="http://serverfault.com/questions/3780/useful-commandline-commands-on-windows" style="border: 0px none rgb(16, 69, 106); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(16, 69, 106); cursor: pointer; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; outline: rgb(16, 69, 106) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; word-wrap: break-word;">
         windows version
        </a>
        of this question, I decided to open a community wiki for the same question under unix, linux, and the like.
       </p>
       <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
        I'll be updating this list with the answers:
       </p>
       <ul style="border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 126px; margin: 0px 0px 14px 30px; text-align: left; width: 630px;">
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          bash
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : exec 3&lt;&gt; /dev/tcp/localhost/80  # Redirect to port 80 of localhost
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          find
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : search for files in a directory hierarchy
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          htop
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : interactive process viewer, similar to top
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          xargs
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : build and execute command lines from standard input
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          tmux
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : detachable, re-attachable command line sessions
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          apropos
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : find relevant man pages
         </span>
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <b>
          vmstat
         </b>
         <span style="font-weight: normal;">
          : See the state of your system
         </span>
        </li>
       </ul>
       <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
        Websites:
       </p>
       <ul style="border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 36px; margin: 0px 0px 14px 30px; text-align: left; width: 630px;">
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         commandlinefu.com
        </li>
        <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         serverfault.com
        </li>
       </ul>
       <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 36px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
        Keyboard shortcuts:
 - Ctrl T (BSD specific): send SIGINFO to a running program
 - Magic SesRq key (Linux specific): en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magic_SysRq_key
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
      </div>

            Save a file you edited in vim without the needed permissions
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="description" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 54px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 54px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            I often forget to sudo before editing a file I don't have write permissions on. When you come to save that file and get the infamous "E212: Can't open file for writing", just issue that vim command in order to save the file without the need to save it to a temp file and then copy it back again.
           </p>

           <a href="http://www.commandlinefu.com/commands/view/1132/mtr-better-than-traceroute-and-ping-combined" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 13px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px;" title="Find out what others think of this command">
            mtr, better than traceroute and ping combined
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="description" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 72px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 18px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            mtr  combines  the  functionality  of the traceroute and ping programs in a single network diagnostic tool.
           </p>
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 54px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            As mtr starts, it investigates the network connection between the host  mtr  runs  on  and HOSTNAME.   by  sending  packets with purposly low TTLs. It continues to send packets with low TTL, noting the response time of the intervening routers.  This allows  mtr  to  print the  response  percentage  and response times of the internet route to HOSTNAME.  A sudden increase in packetloss or response time is often an indication of a bad (or  simply  over?loaded) link.
           </p>
          </div>

           <a href="http://www.commandlinefu.com/commands/view/1551/place-the-argument-of-the-most-recent-command-on-the-shell" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 13px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px;" title="Find out what others think of this command">
            Place the argument of the most recent command on the shell
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="description" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 110px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 18px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            When typing out long arguments, such as:
           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px;">
            cp file.txt /var/www/wp-content/uploads/2009/03/
           </code>
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 18px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            You can put that argument on your command line by holding down the ALT key and pressing the period '.' or by pressing &lt;ESC&gt; then the period '.'. For example:
           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px;">
            cd 'ALT+.'
           </code>
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 36px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">
            would put '/var/www/wp-content/uploads/2009/03/ as my argument. Keeping pressing 'ALT+.' to cycle through arguments of your commands starting from most recent to oldest. This can save a ton of typing.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="options" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 14px; margin: 3px 0px 0px; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; width: 924px;">

           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px;">
            $ cat wikisole.sh
           </code>

           </p>

            #!/bin/sh
           </code>

           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px;">
            dig +short txt ${1}.wp.dg.cx
           </code>

      </div>

      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>

        Backup and Restore MySQL Database Using mysqldump
       </a>
      </div>

     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1085">
       <pre style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; clear: both; color: rgb(17, 17, 17); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 17.984375px; font-family: Consolas, 'Andale Mono', Monaco, Courier, 'Courier New', Verdana, sans-serif; height: 51px; overflow: auto; padding: 8px 11px; white-space: pre; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
        <strong style="border: 0px none rgb(17, 17, 17); color: rgb(17, 17, 17); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 12px; line-height: 17.984375px; font-family: Consolas, 'Andale Mono', Monaco, Courier, 'Courier New', Verdana, sans-serif; outline: rgb(17, 17, 17) none 0px; white-space: pre;">
         backup:
        </strong>
        # mysqldump -u root -p[root_password] [database_name] &gt; dumpfilename.sql
        <strong style="border: 0px none rgb(17, 17, 17); color: rgb(17, 17, 17); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 12px; line-height: 17.984375px; font-family: Consolas, 'Andale Mono', Monaco, Courier, 'Courier New', Verdana, sans-serif; outline: rgb(17, 17, 17) none 0px; white-space: pre;">
         restore:
        </strong>
        # mysql -u root -p[root_password] [database_name] &lt; dumpfilename.sql
       </pre>

   <div class="snippet" data-id="1106" style="width:666px; height:214px; top:1830px; left:674px; min-height:20px; z-index:307;">
    <div class="snippet-content">
     <div class="toolbar toolbar-top">
      <a class="remove-snippet" data-id="1106" href="#">
       <i class="icon-remove">
       </i>
      </a>
      <div class="title-holder">
       <a class="origin-title" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/426272/how-to-test-internet-connection-speed-from-command-line">
        linux - How to test Internet connection speed from command line? - Stack Overflow
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1106">
       <div class="post-text" style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 208px; text-align: left;">
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 36px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Old question, though this solution is missing from the answers.
You could use
         <a href="http://iperf.sourceforge.net/" style="border: 0px none rgb(0, 119, 204); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(0, 119, 204); cursor: pointer; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; outline: rgb(0, 119, 204) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; word-wrap: break-word;">
          iperf
         </a>
         to test the speed between two machines, since 'iperf' was designed to measure bandwidth.
        </p>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         on machine1 (host, this one will receive)
        </p>
        <pre style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; max-height: 600px; overflow: auto; padding: 5px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; width: 650px; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; text-align: left; white-space: pre; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          iperf -s -p 65000
         </code>
        </pre>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         on machine2 (client, this one will upload)
        </p>
        <pre style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; max-height: 600px; overflow: auto; padding: 5px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; width: 650px; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; text-align: left; white-space: pre; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          iperf -c [ip of server] -p 65000
         </code>
        </pre>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Reverse the machines to test the other way (upload-&gt;download or vice versa).
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

   <div class="snippet" data-id="1300" style="width:666px; height:1473px; top:3736px; left:38px; min-height:20px; z-index:424;">
    <div class="snippet-content">
     <div class="toolbar toolbar-top">
      <a class="remove-snippet" data-id="1300" href="#">
       <i class="icon-remove">
       </i>
      </a>
      <div class="title-holder">
       <a class="origin-title" href="http://mmb.pcb.ub.es/~carlesfe/unix/tricks.txt">
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1300">
       <pre style="word-wrap: break-word; white-space: pre-wrap; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: normal; font-family: monospace; height: 1425px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; widows: auto;">
        I have marked with a * those which I think are absolutely essential
Items for each section are sorted by oldest to newest. Come back soon for more!

BASH
* In bash, 'ctrl-r' searches your command history as you type
- Add "set -o vi" in your ~/.bashrc to make use the vi keybindings instead
  of the Emacs ones. Takes some time to get used to, but it's fantastic!
- Input from the commandline as if it were a file by replacing 
  'command &lt; file.in' with 'command &lt;&lt;&lt; "some input text"'
- '^' is a sed-like operator to replace chars from last command 
  'ls docs; ^docs^web^' is equal to 'ls web'. The second argument can be empty.
* '!!:n' selects the nth argument of the last command, and '!$' the last arg
  'ls file1 file2 file3; cat !!:1-2' shows all files and cats only 1 and 2
- More in-line substitutions: http://tiny.cc/ecv0cw
- 'nohup ./long_script &amp;' to leave stuff in background even if you logout
- 'cd -' change to the previous directory you were working on
- 'ctrl-x ctrl-e' opens an editor to work with long or complex command lines
* Use traps for cleaning up bash scripts on exit http://tiny.cc/traps
* 'shopt -s cdspell' automatically fixes your 'cd folder' spelling mistakes


PSEUDO ALIASES FOR COMMONLY USED LONG COMMANDS
- function lt() { ls -ltrsa "$@" | tail; }
- function psgrep() { ps axuf | grep -v grep | grep "$@" -i --color=auto; }
- function fname() { find . -iname "*$@*"; }


VIM
- ':set spell' activates vim spellchecker. Use ']s' and '[s' to move between
  mistakes, 'zg' adds to the dictionary, 'z=' suggests correctly spelled words
- check my .vimrc http://tiny.cc/qxzktw and here http://tiny.cc/kzzktw for more


TOOLS
* 'htop' instead of 'top'
- 'ranger' is a nice console file manager for vi fans
- Use 'apt-file' to see which package provides that file you're missing
- 'dict' is a commandline dictionary
- Learn to use 'find' and 'locate' to look for files
- Compile your own version of 'screen' from the git sources. Most versions
  have a slow scrolling on a vertical split or even no vertical split at all
* 'trash-cli' sends files to the trash instead of deleting them forever. 
  Be very careful with 'rm' or maybe make a wrapper to avoid deleting '*' by
  accident (e.g. you want to type 'rm tmp*' but type 'rm tmp *')
- 'file' gives information about a file, as image dimensions or text encoding
- 'awk '!x[$0]++'' to check for duplicate lines
- 'echo start_backup.sh | at midnight' starts a command at the specified time
- Pipe any command over 'column -t' to nicely align the columns
* Google 'magic sysrq' and learn how to bring you machine back from the dead
- 'diff --side-by-side fileA.txt fileB.txt | pager' to see a nice diff
* 'j.py' http://tiny.cc/62qjow remembers your most used folders and is an 
  incredible substitute to browse directories by name instead of 'cd' 
- 'dropbox_uploader.sh' http://tiny.cc/o2qjow is a fantastic solution to 
  upload by commandline via Dropbox's API if you can't use the official client
- learn to use 'pushd' to save time navigating folders (j.py is better though)
- if you liked the 'psgrep' alias, check 'pgrep' as it is far more powerful
* never run 'chmod o+x * -R', capitalize the X to avoid executable files. If
  you want _only_ executable folders: 'find . -type d -exec chmod g+x {} \;'
- 'xargs' gets its input from a pipe and runs some command for each argument


NETWORKING
- Don't know where to start? SMB is usually better than NFS for most cases.
  'sshfs_mount' is not really stable, any network failure will be troublesome
- 'python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8080' shares all the files in the current 
  folder over HTTP, port 8080
- 'ssh -R 12345:localhost:22 server.com "sleep 1000; exit"' forwards 
  server.com's port 12345 to your local ssh port, even if you machine 
  is not externally visible on the net. 
  Now you can 'ssh localhost -p 12345' from server.com and you will 
  log into your machine. 
  'sleep' avoids getting kicked out from server.com for inactivity
* Read on 'ssh-keygen' to avoid typing passwords every time you ssh
- 'socat TCP4-LISTEN:1234,fork TCP4:192.168.1.1:22' forwards your port
  1234 to another machine's port 22. Very useful for quick NAT redirection.
* Configure postfix to use your personal Gmail account as SMTP:
  http://tiny.cc/n5k0cw. Now you can send emails from the command line.
  'echo "Hello, User!" | mail user@domain.com'
- Some tools to monitor network connections and bandwith:
  'lsof -i' monitors network connections in real time
  'iftop' shows bandwith usage per *connection*
  'nethogs' shows the bandwith usage per *process*
* Use this trick on .ssh/config to directly access 'host2' which is on a private 
  network, and must be accessed by ssh-ing into 'host1' first
  Host host2
      ProxyCommand ssh -T host1 'nc %h %p'
  	  HostName host2
* Pipe a compressed file over ssh to avoid creating large temporary .tgz files
  'tar cz folder/ | ssh server "tar xz"' or even better, use 'rsync'

                                     -~-

        scripting - Repeat a unix command every x seconds forever - Unix and Linux
       </a>

     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1307">
       <div class="post-text" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height: 227px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; widows: auto;">
        <p style="border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height: 22px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Try the
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border: 0px none rgb(34, 34, 34); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: 20px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(34, 34, 34) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          watch
         </code>
         command.
        </p>
        <pre style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: 20px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; height: 40px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; max-height: 600px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow: auto; padding: 5px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; widows: auto; width: 650px; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border: 0px none rgb(34, 34, 34); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: 20px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(34, 34, 34) none 0px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; widows: auto; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          Usage: watch [-dhntv] [--differences[=cumulative]] [--help] [--interval=&lt;n&gt;] 
             [--no-title] [--version] &lt;command&gt;`
         </code>
        </pre>
        <p style="border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         So that:
        </p>
        <pre style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: 20px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; max-height: 600px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow: auto; padding: 5px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; widows: auto; width: 650px; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border: 0px none rgb(34, 34, 34); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 13px; line-height: 20px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(34, 34, 34) none 0px; text-align: left; white-space: pre; widows: auto; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          watch -n1  command
         </code>
        </pre>
        <p style="border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         will run the command every second, forever.
        </p>
        <p style="border: 0px none rgb(51, 51, 51); border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(51, 51, 51) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         OP has asked for link to OS X version of watch:
         <a href="http://www.macports.org/" style="border: 0px none rgb(21, 86, 128); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(21, 86, 128); cursor: pointer; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(21, 86, 128) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word;">

   <div class="snippet" data-id="1332" style="width:858px; height:69px; top:1522px; left:667px; min-height:20px; z-index:464;">
    <div class="snippet-content">

      <div class="title-holder">
       <a class="origin-title" href="http://jeroenjanssens.com/2013/08/16/quickly-navigate-your-filesystem-from-the-command-line.html">
        Quickly navigate your filesystem from the command-line
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1542">
       <h2 style="color: rgb(17, 17, 17); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 600; font-size: 28px; line-height: 48px; font-family: 'Cabin Condensed', sans-serif; height: 48px; orphans: auto; text-align: justify; widows: auto;">
        Quickly navigate your filesystem from the command-line
       </h2>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="toolbar toolbar-bottom">
      <div class="snip-settings">
      </div>
      <div class="resize-handle">
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
   <div class="snippet" data-id="1633" style="width:666px; height:364px; top:3487px; left:1181px; min-height:20px; z-index:427;">
    <div class="snippet-content">
     <div class="toolbar toolbar-top">
      <a class="remove-snippet" data-id="1633" href="#">
       <i class="icon-remove">
       </i>
      </a>
      <div class="title-holder">
       <a class="origin-title" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/73319/duplicate-a-whole-line-in-vim">
        Duplicate a whole line in Vim - Stack Overflow
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="content-html">
      <div id="content-1633">
       <div class="post-text" style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 358px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word;">
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Normal mode: see other answers.
        </p>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         The
         <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ex_%28text_editor%29" style="border: 0px none rgb(0, 119, 204); border-collapse: collapse; color: rgb(0, 119, 204); cursor: pointer; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(0, 119, 204) none 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word;">
          Ex
         </a>
         way:
        </p>
        <ul style="border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 120px; margin: 0px 0px 14px 30px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :t.
          </code>
          will duplicate the line,
         </li>
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :t 7
          </code>
          will copy it after line 7,
         </li>
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 40px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :,+t0
          </code>
          will copy current and next line at the beginning of the file (
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           ,+
          </code>
          is a synonym for the range
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           .,.+1
          </code>
          ),
         </li>
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 40px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :1,t$
          </code>
          will copy lines from beginning till cursor position to the end (
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           1,
          </code>
          is a synonym for the range
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           1,.
          </code>
          ).
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         If you need to move instead of copying, use
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :m
         </code>
         instead of
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :t
         </code>
         .
        </p>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         This can be really powerful if you combine it with
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :g
         </code>
         or
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :v
         </code>
         :
        </p>
        <ul style="border-collapse: collapse; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 58px; margin: 0px 0px 14px 30px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :v/foo/m$
          </code>
          will move all lines not matching the pattern foo to the end of the file.
         </li>
         <li style="border-collapse: collapse; display: list-item; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 38px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 630px; word-wrap: break-word;">
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           :+,$g/^\s*class\s\+\i\+/t.
          </code>
          will copy all subsequent lines of the form
          <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
           class xxx
          </code>
          right after the cursor.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p style="border-collapse: collapse; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Arial, 'Liberation Sans', 'DejaVu Sans', sans-serif; height: 20px; margin: 0px 0px 14px; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; text-align: left; widows: auto; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Reference:
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :help range
         </code>
         ,
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :help :t
         </code>
         ,
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :help :g
         </code>
         ,
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :help :m
         </code>
         and
         <code style="background-image: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-origin: padding-box; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); background-size: auto; border-collapse: collapse; display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, 'Lucida Console', 'Liberation Mono', 'DejaVu Sans Mono', 'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono', 'Courier New', monospace, serif; orphans: auto; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 1px 5px; text-align: left; widows: auto; word-wrap: break-word; background-position: 0% 0%; background-repeat: repeat repeat;">
          :help :v
         </code>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

            </a>

            <a class="vote-button" href="javascript:void(0)" id="vote-down-1551" style="border: 0px none rgb(38, 164, 0); color: rgb(38, 164, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(38, 164, 0) none 0px; widows: auto;">
             Down
            </a>

          <div class="summary" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 15px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 17px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">
           <a href="http://www.commandlinefu.com/commands/view/1551/place-the-argument-of-the-most-recent-command-on-the-shell" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 13px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto;" title="Find out what others think of this command">
            Place the argument of the most recent command on the shell
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="description" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 128px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 18px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">
            When typing out long arguments, such as:
           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px; widows: auto;">
            cp file.txt /var/www/wp-content/uploads/2009/03/
           </code>
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 36px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">
            You can put that argument on your command line by holding down the ALT key and pressing the period '.' or by pressing &lt;ESC&gt; then the period '.'. For example:
           </p>
           <code style="border: 0px none rgb(6, 255, 0); color: rgb(6, 255, 0); display: inline; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 11px; line-height: 18px; font-family: monospace; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(6, 255, 0) none 0px; widows: auto;">
            cd 'ALT+.'
           </code>
           <p style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 18px; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 36px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">
            would put '/var/www/wp-content/uploads/2009/03/ as my argument. Keeping pressing 'ALT+.' to cycle through arguments of your commands starting from most recent to oldest. This can save a ton of typing.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="options" style="border: 0px none rgb(170, 170, 170); color: rgb(170, 170, 170); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', sans-serif, verdana; height: 14px; margin: 3px 0px 0px; orphans: auto; outline: rgb(170, 170, 170) none 0px; widows: auto; width: 870px;">

           </p>
